Crossing the Bar   Sunset and evening star, And one clear call for me! And may there be no moaning of the bar, When I put out to sea,  But such a tide as moving seems asleep, Too full for sound and foam, When that which drew from out the boundless deep Turns again home. Tennyson

I saw Prince Philip and the Queen when I was quite young. they were on a train travelling thru the city I lived in Brantford ontario and my Grandfather took my brothers and I to watch the train to catch a glimps of the royal couple. the train was travelling past us and when the rear car of the train passed the Prince and the queen were standing on the back of the train and my Grandfather yelled out Philip and the prince turned and look a bit bewildered and saw us beside the tracks and said "oh hello there" and smiled and waved at us like we were old friends. I think that made my grandfathers day when that happened and I can still remember the smile on both my grandfathers and the prince's face.
